${{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = spatial background metric
${{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j$ = difference of spatial metric and spatial background metric
${{{ \gamma} _i} _j} = {{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} + {{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j}}$ = spatial metric

${{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial background metric derivative
${{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = difference of spatial metric derivative and spatial background metric derivative, hyperbolic state variable
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}$ = spatial metric derivative
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{{{{ d} _k} _i} _j}}}$

${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ d} _k} _i} _j} = {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}$

${{{ b} ^i} _j} = {{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}}$
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

connections:
${{{{ \Gamma} _i} _j} _k} = {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _i} _k} _{,j}}} - {{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,i}}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \Gamma} _i} _k} _j} + {{{{ \Gamma} _j} _k} _i}}$

${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{\frac{1}{2}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{-{{{{ \gamma} _j} _k} _{,m}}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _j} _{,k}} + {{{{ \gamma} _m} _k} _{,j}}}\right)}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \Gamma} ^i} _j} _k} = {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^m}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _j} - {{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _j} _k}} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _j} _m} _k} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _m} _j} - {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _j} _k}}}\right)}}}$

metric inverse partial:
${{\left( {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}\right)} _{,k}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} _l} _i}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} = {0}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \gamma} _l} _m} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{2}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}\right)}}}$
${{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}} = {-{{{2}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{\left({{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m} + {{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}\right)}}}}$

$\alpha$ = lapse

log lapse derivative:
${{ a} _i} = {{ \alpha} _{,i}}$
${{ a} _i} = {{ \alpha} _{,i}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{ a} _i}$

Bona-Masso lapse evolution:
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \alpha} _{,i}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}}} - {{{{\alpha}^{2}}} {{f}} {{\left({{{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{\Theta}}}}\right)}}}}$
using 1+log slicing: ${f} = {\frac{2}{\alpha}}$
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{{ \alpha} _{,i}}} {{{ \beta} ^i}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{ a} _i}$
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}$

hyperbolic alpha var time evolution
${{{ \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}}}}$
using ${{{ \alpha} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{ { \alpha} _{,k}} _{,t}}$ ; ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{ a} _i}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}}$

${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _i} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}}$
using ${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$

metric evolution:
${{{{ \gamma} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{{{{-2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}} + {{{ \beta} _i} _{,j}} + {{{ \beta} _j} _{,i}}} - {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \Gamma} _k} _i} _j}}}}$

metric delta evolution

metric partial delta evolution:
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,t}} _{,k}} = {{{-{{{2}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l} _{,k}}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}}$

${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{-{{{2}} {{{ \alpha} _{,k}}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ \beta} ^l} _{,k}}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}}\right)}}$
using ${{ \alpha} _{,i}} = {{ a} _i}$ ; ${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}} = {{{ b} ^i} _j}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{-{{{2}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}}\right)}}$
using ${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}} = {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,l}}$
${{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{\frac{1}{2}}{\left({{{-{{{2}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _l}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _i}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _j} _l}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _l}} {{{{{ b} ^l} _i} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _i} _j} _{,k}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j} _{,l}}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}}}\right)}}$

Riemann curvature

${{{ Z} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{ Z} _k} _{,l}}}} + {{{{ Z} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}}} + {{{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{{ K} _k} _l} _{,m}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _n} _l}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^n} _k} _m}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _k} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{{ \Gamma} ^n} _l} _m}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{{{{ K} _m} _n} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _m} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^n}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _p}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _m} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^p} ^n}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _p}}} + {{{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ Z} _m}} {{{{ K} _k} _l}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}}}} - {{{8}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\pi}} \cdot {{{ S} _k}}}} - {{{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}}}$

${{{ Z} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{ Z} _k} _{,l}}}} + {{{{ Z} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}}} + {{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{{ K} _k} _l} _{,m}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _n} _l}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _p} _m}}}} - symmetrizing indexes
${{{ Z} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{ \beta} ^l}} {{{{ Z} _k} _{,l}}}} + {{{{ Z} _l}} {{{{ b} ^l} _k}}} + {{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{{ K} _k} _l} _{,m}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _m} _p}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _m} _k} _p}}}} + {{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _p} _k} _m}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _p} _m}}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _m} _p} _k}}}} + {{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _l} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _p} _k} _m}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _k} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _l} _m} _p}}}} + {{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _k} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _p} _l} _m}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _k} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _l} _p} _m}}}} + {{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _k} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _p} _l} _m}}} - {{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^n}} {{{{{ K} _m} _n} _{,k}}}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _m} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _p}}} + {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _m} _n}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}} {{{{ \gamma} ^n} ^p}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _p}}} + {{{{{{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ Z} _m}} {{{{ K} _k} _l}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^m}}}} - {{{8}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{\pi}} \cdot {{{ S} _k}}}} - {{{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}}}$

Bona-Masso shift evolution:
${{{ \beta} ^i} _{,t}} = {{{ B} ^i} + {{{{ \beta} ^j}} {{{{ \beta} ^i} _{,j}}}}}$

hyperbolic shift $B^i$ evolution:
${{{ B} ^i} _{,t}} = {{{{{{ \beta} ^j}} {{{{ B} ^i} _{,j}}}} - {{{\eta}} \cdot {{{ B} ^i}}}} + {{{\frac{3}{4}}} {{\bar{\Lambda}}}}}$

as a system:
${{ \alpha} _{,t}} = {{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{ a} _i}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{\alpha}}}}$
${{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _j} _{,t}} = {{-{{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _i} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _i} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _j}}} + {{{{{ \hat{\gamma}} _j} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _i}}} + {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{\gamma}} _j} _k}} {{{{ b} ^k} _i}}} + {{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} + {{{{2}} {{{ \beta} ^k}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _i} _j}}} - {{{2}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _t} _i} _j}}}}}$
${{{ a} _k} _{,t}} = {{{{{ a} _i}} {{{{ b} ^i} _k}}} + {{{{{{ \beta} ^i}} {{{{ a} _k} _{,i}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ a} _k}} {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}}}} - {{{2}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ \gamma} ^i} ^j}} {{{{{ K} _i} _j} _{,k}}}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \hat{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{{ K} _i} _j}} {{{{ \gamma} ^l} ^i}} {{{{ \gamma} ^m} ^j}} {{{{{ \overset{\Delta}{d}} _k} _l} _m}}} + {{{4}} {{\alpha}} \cdot {{{ \Theta} _{,k}}}} + {{{4}} {{\Theta}} \cdot {{{ a} _k}}}}$
